# npmi_train Option Testing Log

Testing with 1000 lines corpus.

## Testing with Word Unit 

```
$ time python ./myword.py npmi_train -lr "1,3" -tr "0.1,0.3" -fr "1,3" ./corpus2.1k
```

```

## Prepare Character Segmented Corpus

```
$ ./char-segmentation.sh ./corpus2.1k > ./corpus2.1k.char
$ head -n 3 ./corpus2.1k.char

## Testing with Character Unit 

```
$ time python ./myword.py npmi_train -lr "1,3" -tr "0.1,0.3" -fr "1,3" ./corpus2.1k.char 
```

$ head -n 3 ./corpus2.1k.char.*.seg
